        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2445530133" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16348957773266339153"><b>3 Stars</b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This was enjoyable in its own way, but I'm sad that I'm part of the minority yet again. I wanted to step outside my box again, and I definitely did with this one! It just felt way too insta and I didn't like the way the h turned all preachy about ev-ery-thing! I struggled a good bit with her for especially the second half of the book. I liked the H though! I really liked his interactions with the h's children. I actually was more intrigued with some of the side characters</span>
  <span id="freeText16348957773266339153" style="display:none"><b>3 Stars</b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>This was enjoyable in its own way, but I'm sad that I'm part of the minority yet again. I wanted to step outside my box again, and I definitely did with this one! It just felt way too insta and I didn't like the way the h turned all preachy about ev-ery-thing! I struggled a good bit with her for especially the second half of the book. I liked the H though! I really liked his interactions with the h's children. I actually was more intrigued with some of the side characters than I was by the h by the end of it. Overall, it was an okay read.<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Lisa and Grim's story. Lisa finds herself on an alien ship with 11 other human females in transport to a new group of planets that are in desperate need for females. Grim is a king and second in command of the planets, but he has been deemed unfit to the females and will not be able to create his own much desired family. When Lisa reveals that she has children left behind in Earth and must go back, she agrees to "join" with Grim in exchange for her and her children's safety in the new worlds. After spending more time together, they fall in love with each other. There's is a good bit of political drama between the rulers of the planets, some sexy and sweet times...and they get a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between focusing mainly on Lisa and Grim in 3rd person narrative, but it did have sections that focused on side characters as well.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good for the most part. It did feel like it dragged a little here and there, but never to the point that I felt the need to skim.<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> Yes! Way to insta for my liking TBH. At around 20ish% the h was already declaring her love for the H, and I didn't fully understand the progression into stronger feelings.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Grim. I liked him. I appreciated how he cared for people.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 2.5 stars. Lisa. She got on my nerves with her entitlement thing she had going on. I think I get what the author was trying to do, but it got old quick.<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low, no tissues needed<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b> Not really <br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story (more in first third of book then fizzles out)<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ There is an OW that the H was going to "join" with before the h was in the picture that causes some drama for the couple  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Separation:</b> No, once they're together they stay together.<br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Loss of spouse to cancer (h off page), h had 2 children with dead husband, kidnapping/violence/assault/attempted rape/murder (on and off page), and mentions of rape (side character off page)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> This had alright closure with what I would call a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have pushing away<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse by mcs<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer719044843" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6322576191940188426">almost 5 stars<br/><br/>I hadn't read anything by this author before but when I saw that this book was ranked similarly to sci-fi romance books I'd read, I decide to try a sample then ended up purchasing it. <br/><br/>At it's heart, this is an enjoyable story if interactions between alien men and earth women are what you're wanting to read. Mars men want and need Earth women - favorite trope of mine. <br/><br/>The characters, plot and details are strongly developed and come together well. Grim, Lisa and their daughters creat</span>
  <span id="freeText6322576191940188426" style="display:none">almost 5 stars<br /><br />I hadn't read anything by this author before but when I saw that this book was ranked similarly to sci-fi romance books I'd read, I decide to try a sample then ended up purchasing it. <br /><br />At it's heart, this is an enjoyable story if interactions between alien men and earth women are what you're wanting to read. Mars men want and need Earth women - favorite trope of mine. <br /><br />The characters, plot and details are strongly developed and come together well. Grim, Lisa and their daughters create their happy ending, learning about each other and their cultures as the book progresses. The secondary characters are appealing. I'd love to read Kim and Wray's story sometime and see some of the other women find happiness as they shake up alien culture.<br /><br />Word selection, grammar are not yet M.K.'s strength but will hopefully improve with time and practice. <br /><br />The main reason for the 4 stars rather than 5 stars is the use of present tense throughout the story. Prior to this story, I would have said that tense didn't matter and that I primarily read for well developed characters and plot. But I did find the present tense jarring, creating a barrier against more complete submersion in the story. <br /><br />Despite this, I have purchased M.K.'s other story, Cassandra's Challenge even though it also has the same tense issues. As long as plot and characters are interesting, I would purchase and read M.K stories in the future. <br /><br />cross-posted amazon, goodreads, shelfari<br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1499423392" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16891027749524397337">One day I was looking for something light and simple, something that wouldn't require too much of my limited attention and funny. I needed a break from complicated plots and emotional overload so I picked up Grim. And it delivered. It's hilarious with all those miscommunication between the main characters. If you're looking for a lot of sex, however, this is not for you. Sure there are a couple of explicit scenes but most of the time it's just said that they've had sex. The book is full of clich</span>
  <span id="freeText16891027749524397337" style="display:none">One day I was looking for something light and simple, something that wouldn't require too much of my limited attention and funny. I needed a break from complicated plots and emotional overload so I picked up Grim. And it delivered. It's hilarious with all those miscommunication between the main characters. If you're looking for a lot of sex, however, this is not for you. Sure there are a couple of explicit scenes but most of the time it's just said that they've had sex. The book is full of clichés. Actually the book is one big cliché. So if you don't like a repeat of pretty much any other book with a similar trope you've ever read steer clear of this one. The characters were cute and I came to care for most of them but were so unbelievable that I was thinking of giving up for a while. And the thing that really annoyed me and the reason why this is a 3 star rating is the total lack of editing - spelling and grammar mistakes galore. Dear authors, make sure your books get the proper attention before publishing, cause mistakes like these lower the quality of a book and make a lot of readers to give up and never pick something written by you again.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1286979865" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2911265104510280912">I have attempted this book for a couple days now but sadly could not finish.<br/><br/>I am not a fan of the present tense writing at all. And this story was present tense. For me I couldn't feel any depth to the story cause it was happening "now". The story had some crazy POV switching going on (One sentence is the heroines pov than the next is the heros pov, than it could be another characters pov). There are a lot of authors that do this, its not bad or anything but to me it starts getting confusing. <br/><br/>Th</span>
  <span id="freeText2911265104510280912" style="display:none">I have attempted this book for a couple days now but sadly could not finish.<br /><br />I am not a fan of the present tense writing at all. And this story was present tense. For me I couldn't feel any depth to the story cause it was happening "now". The story had some crazy POV switching going on (One sentence is the heroines pov than the next is the heros pov, than it could be another characters pov). There are a lot of authors that do this, its not bad or anything but to me it starts getting confusing. <br /><br />The book needs edited. <br /><br />All that aside, of what I read, Grim was a sweet character. Main characters fell in love really quick. <br /></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2338792200" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12980149314269600597"><blockquote>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499162225ra/23198382.gif' width='200' height='150' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/>The owls's reaction sums up mine when I was Halfway through <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18468256.Grim__Tornians___1_' title='Grim (Tornians, #1) by M.K. Eidem' rel='nofollow noopener'>Grim</a>. I was not expecting this book to be a good read because I have been really prone to falling for flashy descriptions(a lot), recently. (ahem ahem <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10439221.Claimed__Brides_of_the_Kindred___1_' title='Claimed (Brides of the Kindred, #1) by Evangeline Anderson' rel='nofollow noopener'>Claimed</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/31247842.Wicked_Fall__The_Wicked_Horse___1_' title='Wicked Fall (The Wicked Horse, #1) by Sawyer Bennett' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wicked Fall</a> could belong to the said lot).<br/><br/>Grim Vasteri is overprotective, a king and an alpha male to boot. He loves his Lisa and the kids and is willing to die for them. I was very surprised at how Lisa handles being kidnapped and then later adjusts to her new life, all for </span>
  <span id="freeText12980149314269600597" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1499162225ra/23198382.gif" width="200" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>The owls's reaction sums up mine when I was Halfway through <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18468256.Grim__Tornians___1_" title="Grim (Tornians, #1) by M.K. Eidem" rel="nofollow noopener">Grim</a>. I was not expecting this book to be a good read because I have been really prone to falling for flashy descriptions(a lot), recently. (ahem ahem <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10439221.Claimed__Brides_of_the_Kindred___1_" title="Claimed (Brides of the Kindred, #1) by Evangeline Anderson" rel="nofollow noopener">Claimed</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/31247842.Wicked_Fall__The_Wicked_Horse___1_" title="Wicked Fall (The Wicked Horse, #1) by Sawyer Bennett" rel="nofollow noopener">Wicked Fall</a> could belong to the said lot).<br><br>Grim Vasteri is overprotective, a king and an alpha male to boot. He loves his Lisa and the kids and is willing to die for them. I was very surprised at how Lisa handles being kidnapped and then later adjusts to her new life, all for the sake of her children. While it didn't hurt that Grim was loyal to a boot, I loved how he had his own doubts about being unfit because of the Scarring. <br><br>Here is why I am giving only 3.5 stars.<br><br>1. The warriors who have scars are "Unfit". What sort of fricking rule is this? How else are they supposed to fight and defend? Using Rose petal and Velvet Swords? Or just stare the enemies to death, I guess. Major Stupidity if you ask me. <br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1522189331ra/25282498.gif" width="200" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>2. Ok lets say something happens and there is some Scarring. To be such an advanced civilization who has mastered intergalactic space travel, an educator that imparts knowledge to other species, why didn't they just Zap the scarring away? One could probably argue it is to do with honor and protecting what belongs to him. But again 8 against 1? Though he defeated all 8, Grim is still categorized as Unfit. The frick-up fairy is strong with this one.<br><br>3. Again, for such advanced people, they do clean a lot using their hands. Sucks to be them I guess. (Felt like they spoke about it a lot).<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1511025847ra/24477668.gif" width="200" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>4. How no one made the connection of Risa being the bad guy, when she seems to be in every single incident that has happened directly or indirectly. Every Single one. <br><br>Here is why I am giving 3.5 stars.<br><br>1. Loved how Lisa changed everyone and everything in the castle, despite the Tornian Ways, which everyone else seems to follow without question.<br><br>2. Grim scores major brownie points as he always asks and rectifies after every frick up he makes.<br><br>3.Lisa is uber practical and takes charge in the Council meetings and Joining Ceremony.<br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1519740817ra/25131347.gif" width="200" height="150" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>4. The political problems and back stabbings were not too over the top but at the same time realistic.<br><br>5. Grim and Lisa make a good pair :P <br><br>I would love to continue this series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12980149314269600597" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer892509595" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10881662824349645989">I have read this book and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20718586.Wray__Tornians___2_' title='Wray (Tornians, #2) by M.K. Eidem' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1391508426s/20718586.jpg' alt='Wray (Tornians, #2) by M.K. Eidem' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> several times. I decided this time to read Wray first and then read this one. There is a reason I read these books over and over. They are filled with love, acceptance and hope in an alien world. <br/><br/>I love a scarred, tortured hero and Grim is just that. He thinks he is unfit and unworthy when in reality he is just the opposite and what all of the Tornians should want to be like. Lisa and her little girls, Miki and Carly, give him that love and acceptance.<br/><br/>This is reall</span>
  <span id="freeText10881662824349645989" style="display:none">I have read this book and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20718586.Wray__Tornians___2_" title="Wray (Tornians, #2) by M.K. Eidem" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1391508426s/20718586.jpg" alt="Wray (Tornians, #2) by M.K. Eidem" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> several times. I decided this time to read Wray first and then read this one. There is a reason I read these books over and over. They are filled with love, acceptance and hope in an alien world. <br><br>I love a scarred, tortured hero and Grim is just that. He thinks he is unfit and unworthy when in reality he is just the opposite and what all of the Tornians should want to be like. Lisa and her little girls, Miki and Carly, give him that love and acceptance.<br><br>This is really a wonderful book and you cannot go wrong reading this series.<br><br></span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_7203997'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7203997-ral-s-woman"><img alt="Ral&#39;s Woman (Zorn Warriors, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1259343679l/7203997._SY160_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IXZjV0g26SWHxeSB6hn/hEKtYl1SkcGhNW9e7sDkNt9K3JU6VREIN3o9TpDjEtIDRv2EQ/obCUfi7gzvANqBCw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

When local law enforcement couldn\'t find them, she reached out to the most powerful person she knew. The President of the United States, her Uncle.  Two people who have had their lives turned upside down are on a collision course. How these two handled the impact and deal with the aftermath will affect not just them but all the Known Universes. <\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"13174523479213823751\" href=\"#\" This partial loads on almost every page view.  The associated React component makes
a call to SignInPromptController#get to determine if the user should see the sign in interstial.
This is determined by how many signed out pagehits the user has executed an how recently they have
last seen the insterstitial.  If the controller responds indicating the popup should appear, the
